</div><div class="visareqtext"><span id="md_visareq" class="md_visareq" style="color:#ff0033">Applicants must be eligible to work in the specified location</span></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p><strong>UX Designer - Sketch, Invision, Jira | Up To £450 Per Day</strong></p> <p><strong>Berkshire</strong></p> <p><strong>6 month rolling contract</strong></p> <p>Digital Skills are looking for an experienced UX Designer to join our clients CX scrum team in their Berkshire location and help create exceptional and engaging user experiences.</p> <p>Must have worked on digital products with knowledge of UX trends (past, present and predicted). As part of a collaborative team, the UX designer will be expected to apply expertise and insights to deliver the best user experience by exploring different approaches to deliver on business value or to solve multi-channel customer experience problems.</p> <p>This role is ideally suited to designers who want to get stuck into an exciting challenge on a large complex digital programme. You will have good time management and organisation skills, with experience of working directly with clients in a collaborative environment and always be ready to be hands-on.</p> <p><strong>Responsibilities:</strong></p> <ul> <li>Analysing existing processes, artifacts and evaluating their user experience and effectiveness.</li> <li>Assessing the user persona(s), channel (web, mobile, retail) and interaction element of design or workflow.</li> <li>Defining interaction models, user task flows, and UI (user interface) specifications.</li> <li>Create wire-frames &amp; managing design libraries.</li> <li>Communicating scenarios, end-to-end experiences, interaction models, and screen designs to scrum team members and the wider sprint group.</li> <li>Developing and maintaining design wireframes (basic mock-ups of applications) and specifications.</li> <li>Ensuring that wire-frames and other CX deliverables are annotated accordingly using good grammar and syntax.</li> </ul> <p><strong>Skills:</strong></p> <p>You will have an impressive portfolio that demonstrates your skills and expertise across many areas of the UX landscape including:</p> <ul> <li>User Journey mapping and Experience mapping</li> <li>Task &amp; Process analysis</li> <li>Information Architecture</li> <li>Sketching/Scamps</li> <li>Wire-framing</li> <li>UCD Strategy &amp; Persuasive Design Collaboration</li> <li>Good written and verbal skills to communicate complex interaction design concepts at all levels</li> </ul> <p><strong>Tools:</strong></p> <ul> <li>Experienced in using Sketch &amp; Invision</li> <li>Confluence/Jira</li> </ul> <p><strong>Experience:</strong></p> <ul> <li>Great expectation management and collaboration skills across multi-discipline teams</li> <li>Experience scoping timescales and delivering on time</li> <li>Be able to work fairly autonomously.</li> <li>Have previously worked on responsive web projects.</li> <li>Experience of working within a highly governed project.</li> <li>A portfolio that tells a story, not just wireframes and finished visuals. We want to be able to understand what you've done specifically and understand your thinking.</li> <li>Previous working experience in either Telecom/Retail/E-commerce or Digital domain</li> </ul></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">

report testing, ensuring adequate depth and breadth of test coverage.</li><li>Carry out end-to-end, data completeness and quality, regression testing, including standard data validation and ensure data maintains integrity at all stages of transformation (ETL) and data flow.</li><li>Data preparation, data loads for journaling or ETL and processing in test environments.</li><li>Data reconciliation in BI reports by means of reports comparison and by executing SQL queries.</li></ul> <p><strong>Skills required:</strong></p><ul> <li>Software Testing experience within SDLC, preferably You will fulfil a vital part of the digital products team shaping the team of test analysts, and identifying the best techniques, suppliers and technologies for our needs. <br><br>Knowledge, skills &amp; Python</li><li>Has good knowledge of SDLC (Software development life cycle)</li><li>Is proficient in websites, mobile apps, TV apps and API manual testing</li><li>Experience using JIRA or Trello</li><li>Has knowledge of quality assurance processes and procedures</li><li>Has a proactive and flexible approach to work and is comfortable with a dynamic environment with constantly changing priorities</li><li>Is comfortable juggling multiple projects at the same time</li><li>Has a working knowledge of working within an agile project management process</li><li>Strong relationship management and communication skills with the ability to work collaboratively with colleagues across a number of departments and services as necessary</li></ul><p>Key Responsibilities</p><ul><li>Undertake manual testing across all digital products as required, (iOS, Android, website, TV apps) keeping a good record of results, collating and reporting on issues in a clear manner</li><li>Undertake automation testing across mobile platforms, building tests from the ground up.</li><li>With an eye for detail, regression test across all devices as and when necessary</li><li>Raise critical issues with a sense of urgency, following processes set out</li><li>Play a key part in developing the team's automated testing capabilities, using Gherkin and Selenium</li><li>Adopt BDD techniques as part of a standard project workflow processes</li><li>Keep the other team members in regular touch with progress and issues</li><li>Raise bugs with a sense of urgency, as necessary, following through with final testing and go live</li><li>Be familiar with Charles, Wireshark and Android Device Monitor for capturing logs and analysing output</li><li>Manage and action GDPR requests in a timely manner, as required</li></ul><p>This job ad was posted by Salt. This company produce software that <strong>harnesses the Microsoft .NET stack as well as modern visualisation tools</strong> - the result is a highly complex software product capable of providing large companies with better control over their own software applications. <div class="top_detail" id="top_detail"><div class="LeftJobHeaderWrapper" id="LeftJobHeaderWrapper"><h1 id="positiontitle" class="positiontitle"><a href="/HKOl0" id="td_jobpositionlink" title="Technical Architect" target="_blank">Technical Architect</a><!-- job position (and link to another page) --></h1><span id="td_location_salary" class="td_location_salary">Bradford, West Yorkshire</span><!-- location and/or salary (if the job has them) --><span id="td_job_type" class="td_job_type">Permanent</span><!-- job type --><span id="td_posted_date" id="td_addbskt_btn" title="Add this to the job basket" class="nojsbasketbutton jobbasketbutton basketbutton jobitembasket  JIB993527244E75760058" name="JIB993527244E75760058"></a></div></div><div id="detail_2_ph"></div><div id="dataDiv"></div></div><div class="RightJobHeaderWrapper" id="RightJobHeaderWrapper"><div id="logoDiv" class="logoDiv"><a href="/gb/en/Redirect/DirectoryUrl.jsrs?id=F413814574&amp;L=%2fgb%2fen%2fListings%2fEmployers%2fMastek-UK%2f%3flid%3dF413814574" id="md_agency_logo_link" class="md_agency_logo_link" title="View more information about Mastek (UK)"><img src="https://az274887.vo.msecnd.net/images/blank.gif" id="md_agency_logo" class="md_agency_logo right" alt="Mastek (UK)"><!-- job branding logo --></a></div></div><div class="clear">&nbsp;</div></div>
<div class="clear">&nbsp;</div>
<input name="ctl00$jidval" type="hidden" id="jidval" value="993527244E75760058"><div id="JobDetailContainer" style="height: 564px;"><div id="jobDetailScroll_outercontainer" class="jobscrolllist_outercontainer"><div class="customScrollBox"><div class="jsCustomScrollContainer" style="top: 0px;"><div class="jsCustomScrollContent"><div class="main_detail_content"><div id="seemore" class="dv_seemorelink"><a href="/gb/en/JobSearch.aspx?jid=993527244E75760058" id="md_seemorelink" class="md_seemorelink">See more jobs like this</a>
</div><div class="visareqtext"></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p><strong>Duties and responsibilities</strong></p> <ul> <li>In Mastek UK Ltd., the role of Technical Architect is expected to perform an organized and structured analysis of technical issues, and have the ability to transform these inferences into meaningful solutions. For this, the technical architect needs to interface with the client architects and business teams to convert their business requirements into designs that are more tangible for implementation by programmers. Further to this the role also demands the technical architect to be the point of contact for all architect and design-related guidance to support the larger technical team on a day to day basis.</li> <li>Analyzing skills will help investigate issues, to understand the root causes of failures that come up while extending the functionality or supporting an existing application. Collaborate with the business, management and technical teams to ensure resources are utilized in the most efficient manner. In this liaising role also communicate extensively with both technical and non-technical stakeholders. Translate the client's business requirements and use cases, to functional specifications and technical designs. Analyze and validate the Non-Functional Requirements (NFR) for compliance verification, ensures these and all development activities are aligned to the enterprise architecture.</li> <li>As Technical Architect, accountability for all architecture and design decisions, technical sign-off reviews, estimates for new initiatives and road maps. Technical Architect role needs to perform an extensive analysis of the implementation risks, which also helps in a functional review of the dependencies between the interfacing systems. From time to time the role demands to migrate the production systems onto the AWS cloud, empowering the team with the right guidance. Technical Architect needs to be at the forefront, holding accountability for complex technical decisions, ensuring the team remained focused and connected to address critical issues on time.</li> <li>Strategize and innovate on the system architecture to make it future-proof. This necessitates formulating methodologies to optimize it for scalability, stability and performance. Play an active role in the evaluation of the client infrastructure frameworks involving DevOps and cloud, fulfilling their IT priorities to meet business objectives.</li> </ul> <p>Skills, qualifications and experience required to be able to perform the role:</p> <p><strong>Skills</strong></p> <ul> <li>Retail (Supply Chain, Manufacturing, Finance and Logistics) knowledge is essential.</li> <li>Very strong experience working with microservices and event-driven architectures</li> <li>A strong hands-on of AWS products and using these to design services</li> <li>Experience designing solutions using modern engineering techniques including infrastructure-as-code</li> <li>Experience working on consumer-facing digital products</li> <li>Practical experience of designing solutions based upon custom development, Front End API integration and third-party cloud services</li> <li>Excellent knowledge of software and application design and architecture.</li> <li>Excellent knowledge of Java and JavaScript</li> <li>Good understanding of software quality assurance principles.</li> <li>Formal training and certification in Application Architect/System Architect</li> <li>Hands-on skills with Front End Technologies (HTML5, CSS3, jQuery, jQuery Plugins, JSON, and developing cross-platform code).</li> <li>Experience working with different architecture, patterns, frameworks (scripts/queries, batch jobs, troubleshooting Java APIs/services, Java/J2EE, Spring Framework, Web Services</li> </ul> <p><strong>Operating System:</strong> Windows 7, 8</p> <p><strong>Languages &amp; We are a fast paced and forward thinking business so we want to speak to people who are adaptable, agile, ambitious and the best in their field. </p> <p> Responsibilities </p> <ul> <li>Work closely with the client to fully understand their requirements</li> <li>May lead Small to medium size teams (1-6 people) or be a subject matter expert</li> <li>Work closely with our clients to define and develop the best possible solutions</li> <li>Apply your extensive knowledge of manual software testing to provide innovative and cutting edge solutions.</li> <li>Provide expert advice and feedback to our clients</li> <li>It is important that you are both enthusiastic about and possess a strong understanding of software development and a variety of methodologies, especially Agile</li> <li>Ability to work independently</li> <li>Work closely and collaboratively with other teams across the business</li> <li>Be tool agnostic and recommend new processes and techniques to improve the capability of testing for our clients.</li> <li>Produce clear and concise reports and documentation</li> </ul> <p> Essential Skills </p> <ul> <li>Extensive experience across a number of testing disciplines (Mobile, Regression, Web, System, Acceptance, UAT)</li> <li>Experience with test management tools (Team Foundation Server, HP Quality Center, Jira)</li> <li>Experience of working in an Agile development environment (SCRUM, Kanban, DSDM, TDD, BDD)</li> <li>Must have experience of leading teams through the full testing life cycle</li> <li>Willingness to Travel and stay away from home sometimes for extended periods should this be required.</li> <li>Excellent documentation and interpersonal skills</li> <li>Must have a valid work permit for the UK</li> </ul> <p> Desired Skills </p> <ul> <li>Previous experience in a consultancy environment would be beneficial</li> <li>Exposure to Performance and Automation tools would be highly beneficial - (Selenium/Loadrunner/Cucumber/SoapUI/Jmeter)</li> </ul> <p> Working at Ten10 </p> <p>Ten10 has a culture of transparency, communication and respect. We are adept at delivering testing solutions across a broad range of tools, technologies and industries.</p> <p> Progression at Ten10 </p> <p>Ten10 is a consultancy so it is likely you will work across multiple clients, projects and engagements using multiple tools &amp; technologies, which will accelerate your knowledge, skills and career.</p> <p>By empowering our people within our structured multi-level career model, to be both responsible and accountable for their delivery, career and own development, we ensure our people can progress upwards without any limitations other than their own ambition, ability, and attitude.</p> <p> Benefits at Ten10 </p> <p>We also offer a very attractive benefits package which includes (but is not limited to):</p> <ul> <li>Hours: 7.5h per day, 37.5h per week, Flexible Working</li> <li>Holiday: 25 days + 1 day holiday for every extra day worked up to 3 years</li> <li>Technology: Company Laptop, Google Apps &amp; Office 365, Slack</li> <li>Schemes: Bonus, Subsidised Gym, Childcare, Bike to Work, Season Ticket</li> <li>Pension: Contributory matched by employer up to 5%</li> <li>Training: Excellent training and development opportunities are also tailored to you</li> <li>Social: Fridges, Communication Events, Summer &amp; Xmas Parties</li> <li>Health: Health Plan, Death In Service, Critical Illness, Eye Tests</li> <li>AND: a whole lot more! </li></ul></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">

They have a unique suite of products and an even more unique culture.</p><p>Based in the beautiful town of Leamington Spa, their cutting edge, award winning solutions have been used across the production landscape - feature films, TV and commercials. They're now looking for an iOS Developer to join their team.</p><p><strong>What's The Opportunity?</strong></p><p>As an iOS Engineer, you will be responsible for development of iOS and Apple TV apps at PIX. Our apps are used by some of the most creative and visually acute users on the planet - feature film directors, visual effects artists, movie &amp; television producers, and studio executives. PIX is installed at virtually every major studio and production facility so you will have major impact on software that goes into making shows and movies you and your friends likely watch. </p><p>This isn't just a technical role either - you'll get to develop partnerships across the business, including the product, design, infra and developer experience teams. Our apps are used by some of the most creative and visually acute users on the planet - feature film directors, visual effects artists, movie &amp; television producers, and studio executives. PIX is installed at virtually every major studio and production facility so you will have major impact on software that goes into making shows and movies you and your friends likely watch.</p><p><strong>Responsibilities</strong></p><ul><li>Be a key contributing member of the Cocoa development team.</li><li>Design and implement features on one or more PIX applications for iOS and Apple TV.</li><li>Build shared components across applications.</li><li>Specify and develop interfaces to the PIX Service Back End APIs.</li><li>Coordinate with Product teams on feature specification and delivery.</li><li>Coordinate &amp; communicate with local and distributed/overseas team members.</li></ul><p><strong>Requirements</strong></p><ul><li>Degree in Computer Science or equivalent.</li><li>Minimum 2+ years work experience building iOS applications.</li><li>Demonstrated knowledge of Swift, Xcode, and other related technologies.</li><li>Experience with network-based applications and/or frameworks.</li><li>Familiar with development tools such as Git, Jira, Confluence, Jenkins, or equivalents.</li><li>Excellent troubleshooting and problem-solving skills.</li></ul><p><strong>Additional Preferred Experience</strong></p><ul><li>Experience with AVFoundation and/or other multi-media technologies.</li><li>Experience with SwiftUI.</li><li>Experience with Apple TV applications.</li><li>Experience working with distributed/remote teams.</li></ul><p><strong>Benefits</strong></p><p>Competitive salary and bonus programme.</p><p>Private BUPA medical insurance including coverage for spouse and family.</p><p>Life assurance covering 4x basic annual salary.</p><p>Employee equity and pension plan.</p><p>Commitment to professional development.</p><p>Work along no less than 6 Academy and Emmy Award winning technologists!</p><p>We are an equal opportunities employer and welcome applications from all suitably qualified persons regardless of their race, sex, disability, religion/belief, sexual orientation, gender reassignment, marriage and civil partnerships, pregnancy or maternity or age.</p></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">

Joining a high performing team who are building mobile apps, giving you an opportunity to work on products with high visibility within Worldpay whilst delivering new services to our customers.<br><br>How will you add value on a day-today basis?<br>You'll have experience in testing within an IOS and Android multi-product and multi-geography environment. You'll contribute in sprints using automated and manual testing approaches to verify that the delivered solution matches the intended outcome of the Product Owner. <br>You'll maintain knowledge of all products within the Mobile Product Portfolio to shape the approach to testing for the specific components being developed by the agile team. You'll be skilled in both automated and manual approaches and assess which is the best approach whilst following the end to end software development life cycle.<br><br>What will make you the ideal candidate?<br>We are looking for individuals with experience in a mobile testing who has worked as a member in an agile team. Knowledge in mobile device testing for mobile applications and web based applications is key.<br><br>Experience in a manual and automated testing approaches including appropriate tooling for different activities related to the product delivery, for example:<br>o JIRA/Confluence - Product Backlog management<br>o HP ALM - Test Management<br>o Mobile Centre/Appium/Eggplant - Mobile specific tooling<br>o Jenkins/Maven/Nexus - CI/CD tooling<br>o Cucumber - BDD tooling<br><br>Why Worldpay?<br>Worldpay has merged with Vantiv Inc. to create a new global leader in payments. The new Worldpay will have the scale, the reach and the resources to take our success story to another level. This move allows us to expand further into high growth markets, deliver innovation at scale and above all, brings together exceptional talent and a shared passion that will help propel us forward to the next chapter of our collective story.<br>Our technology enables billions of payments to be made each year whether online or in person. Working with customers large and small we help them to take payments quickly, safely and reliably, allowing them to grow their businesses and making your life more convenient in the process.<br> <br></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">

<input name="ctl00$jidval" type="hidden" id="jidval" value="90228190BF48107161"><div id="JobDetailContainer" style="height: 564px;"><div id="jobDetailScroll_outercontainer" class="jobscrolllist_outercontainer"><div class="customScrollBox"><div class="jsCustomScrollContainer" style="top: 0px;"><div class="jsCustomScrollContent"><div class="main_detail_content"><div id="seemore" class="dv_seemorelink"><a href="/gb/en/JobSearch.aspx?jid=90228190BF48107161" id="md_seemorelink" class="md_seemorelink">See more jobs like this</a>
</div><div class="visareqtext"><span id="md_visareq" class="md_visareq" style="color:#ff0033">Applicants must be eligible to work in the specified location</span></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills">Why is our Middleware Support team the next step for you?<br><br>This role sits within our Hosting and Application Services. In this role, you'll be responsible for providing Middleware support for a wide range of Middleware products, including 3rd line BAU support for production and pre-production environments.<br><br>How will you contribute on a day-to-day basis?<br><br>In this role, you'll provide 3rd line Middleware support responsibilities including installation, configuration, maintenance and live support of Middleware services hosted on Linux and Microsoft operating systems in a highly virtualised environment and subject to strict change management and service level agreements. You'll provide high standards of service from a Middleware perspective in terms of service maintenance, new capability requests, fault prevention and resolution. You'll provide technical expertise within the following technologies: Oracle Weblogic, Oracle Fusion products such as ORMB, Documaker, ODI, and Java/J2EE.<br><br>As part of this role, you'll participate in an on-call rota to provide out-of-hours support. You'll take on discretionary projects and engineering tasks and participate in the shaping and continuous improvement for Middleware Support.<br><br>What will make you the right fit for the team?<br>You'll have experience supporting Oracle Fusion Middleware products like Oracle Weblogic (including Coherence &amp; OHS), Oracle Revenue Management &amp; Billing (ORMB), Oracle Documaker, Oracle WebCenter, Oracle OBIEE and Oracle Enterprise Manager. You'll have experience of 3rd level support for business critical production systems, ITIL experience and knowledge of Java/J EE and associated concepts including Object-Oriented and Service-Oriented design. We are looking for strong analytical skills coupled with a methodical approach to fault investigation and resolution, and a service management ethos and disciplined approach to management of support tasks.<br><br>You'll have strong communication and stakeholder management skills, and experience with Service Now and JIRA are ideal.<br><br>How is Worldpay changing the world?<br><br>Worldpay has merged with Vantiv Inc. to create a new global leader in payments. The new Worldpay will have the scale, the reach and the resources to take our success story to another level. This move allows us to expand further into high growth markets, deliver innovation at scale and above all, brings together exceptional talent and a shared passion that will help propel us forward to the next chapter of our collective story.<br><br>Our technology enables billions of payments to be made each year whether online or in person. Working with customers large and small we help them to take payments quickly, safely and reliably, allowing them to grow their businesses and making your life more convenient in the process. <br></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">

You must have demonstratable experience managing the design, development and delivery of large-scale testing engagements across a broad range of platforms.</p> <p>Essential Criteria for the role:</p> <ul> <li>Over 10+ years of testing experience on large Integration programmes </li> <li>Prior experience of establishing large scale Test delivery organization</li> <li>Strong background managing software testing through Test delivery life cycle </li> <li>Experience managing testing teams in complex programmes across geographies</li> <li>Strong experience in business processes, testing methodologies &amp; tools </li> <li>Experience of defining test strategy/Test approach for large scale complex programme</li> <li>Has led testing in multi-technology transformation projects</li> <li>Strong experience of Waterfall, Agile/Scrum and iterative/incremental software delivery</li> <li>Knowledge of some test frameworks and solutions to manage complexity</li> <li>Experience managing E2E testing of ERP Applications</li> <li>Experience in driving detailed test plans, test scripts and test execution</li> <li>Experience in managing Functional, non-Functional, performance testing, Operational testing</li> <li>Experience is automating testing (Selenium)</li> <li>Manage Agile testing using HP QC/JIRA or comparable platforms</li> <li>Strong stakeholder management and excellent communication skills</li> <li>Bachelor's Degree or HNC in Computer Science, Information Systems, or other related field, or equivalent work experience</li> <li>ISTQB Foundation Certification/Testing Certification</li> </ul></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">

It is very important for us to serve our clients to leverage technical advancement and address their business challenges. </p> <p>Our mission is to help our clients to achieve their business goals by providing best-in-class <strong>Seamless Innovative Integration Solutions</strong>. </p> <p>SERES is strengthening their capability to develop comprehensive range of products and services to support financial advisory firms, financial institutions, banks and multinational product companies. In order to achieve this, we are looking forward for talented resources. Here we are inviting you to join our workforce and enjoy the exciting journey in Integration space. </p> <p><strong>Job Title</strong>: Integration Developer</p> <p><strong>Job Location</strong>: London,United Kingdom</p> <p><strong>Salary</strong>: £60,000-£70,000/annum</p> <p>No.of Positions: x2 </p> <p><strong>The Integration Developer roles expects you to</strong></p> <ul> <li>Own the Integration stack development process from requirements gathering to full implementation.</li> <li>As a developer focus on the API &amp; Platforms integration.</li> <li>Monitor, troubleshoot, and resolve problems with monitoring tools such as Geneos, App Dynamics etc used in the Integration landscape.</li> <li>Collaborate with development team to architect efficient and stable production integrations.</li> <li>Document and analyze current business processes and underlying systems/applications.</li> <li>Communicate and collaborate effectively with technical peers (scrum teams) and business users (Product Owners)</li> <li>Form strong working relationships with client teams and across the IT organization.</li> <li>Be able to work in an Agile teams and participate in the regular ceremonies.</li> <li>Provide sizing, effort and delivery estimates for project requests</li> <li>Produce progress reports, articulate risks or issues impeding a successful implementation.</li> <li>Engage in related communities to stay abreast of new tools and development solutions</li> </ul> <p><strong>Key Skills/Knowledge required for Integration Developer Role </strong></p> <p><strong>Competencies:</strong></p> <ul> <li>4+ years of experience as Integration Systems Developer with exposure to technology development projects and the full technology development life cycle.</li> <li>Accomplishment in delivering at least two or more real-world business applications/projects.</li> <li>Expertise with J2EE, knowledgeable on enterprise integration patterns, software design patterns, technologies including but not limited to RESTful web service, high availability, etc.</li> <li>Application Implementation experience using various integration framework/suites - Mule, Apache Camel, Spring etc.</li> <li>Application Integration using Open Source Stack, Java Sprint Boot, C#, .NET and any other open source products</li> <li>Demonstrated proficiency with an object-oriented programming language with design and algorithmic analysis background.</li> <li>Ability to learn new tools and technologies related to the Integration framework and apply them effectively in the solution development.</li> </ul> <p><strong>Soft Skills:</strong></p> <ul> <li>Excellent oral, written communication and Inter-personal skills, both with business customers and with fellow IT professionals (Business Analysts/Product Owners, Project Managers/Scrum Masters and Developers).</li> <li>Ability to present complex technical information in a clear and concise manner to a variety of audiences.</li> <li>Very important to demonstrate a positive team-first attitude</li> <li>Ability to multi-task, prioritize and manage technical issues with strong problem-solving and analytical thinking skills.</li> <li>Strong Work ethic that demonstrate commitment in performing work/assigned tasks with excellence.</li> </ul> <p><strong>Process Skills</strong></p> <ul> <li>Experience in Agile development techniques like Scrum and Test Driven development.</li> <li>Agile delivery experience</li> <li>Experienced in using an iterative process such as SCRUM to deliver engineering projects; experience in continuous improvement to development process.</li> </ul> <p><strong>Technical Skills</strong></p> <ul> <li>Proficiency in Java/J2EE, Spring, Hibernate, Spring Boot, Apache framework such as Camel, Messaging such as AMQ, IBM MQ or Solace.</li> <li>Hands-on experience with usage of Spring Boot and in-depth knowledge Event Driven Architecture.</li> <li>Strong technical development experience with effective coding, code reviews, design patterns, best practices on configuration management and code refactoring.</li> <li>Must have experience in Micro service development and RESTful Web services.</li> <li>Must have experience in using Git, Maven, Sonar and Atlassian tools (Jira and Confluence)</li> <li>Must have experience with Developer testing tools like JUnit, Mokito, Cucumber etc.</li> <li>Must have strong experience with the usage of data storage systems such as Oracle, SQL Server, MongoDB, and Elastic search.</li> <li>Must have an in-depth understanding of database technologies (SQL and NoSQL) as well as API cache design and caching technologies.</li> <li>Must have strong knowledge Integration Platform As Service solutions.</li> <li>Must have strong knowledge of cloud infrastructure, monitoring and orchestration tools.</li> <li>Must have strong knowledge on AWS, Azure and other Cloud solutions.</li> <li>Must have strong knowledge of SOA, REST, JMS, Web Services (JAX-WS, JAX-RS, SOAP, REST), and transfer protocols (HTTP(s), (s)ftp, etc.).</li> <li>Must have experience with using CI/CD technologies such as Jenkins, Bamboo, Travis CI and Drone.</li> <li>Must have good understanding of DevOps and delivering through CI/CD pipelines to production.</li> </ul></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div from </strong><strong>£65,000 - £95,000 Plus Superb Bonus &amp; Benefits Package</strong><br><br> Through business growth and transformation, this hugely successful Insurance corporate is recruiting for a Senior Java Developer to join a team dedicated to the analysis, technical design, development &amp; implementation of new IT Services &amp; systems, including the moving of Java applications into the Cloud.<br><br> Working within the IT team in a collaborative environment and adhering to the latest Agile methodologies, the Senior Java Developer will work closely with product owners, business stakeholders, technical architects, business analysts, test teams, strategic software providers and infrastructure services providers, to deliver high quality, appropriate, reliable solutions to the business and their customers while governing and implementing coding standards. <br><br> Along with strong Java/J2EE skills, the Senior Java Developer will also need experience developing REST API's, Web Services or Micro Services.<br><br> <strong>Responsibilities Include:</strong><br><br> Design, develop, maintain, upgrade, document and deploy software components to deliver high quality solutions to the business and their customers that align with IT strategy, integrate with the existing IT architecture and technology and contribute to continuous improvement of the IT systems<br><br> As a Senior Developer you will be expected to lead, mentor, share knowledge with and offer technical guidance to less experienced members of the development team and take responsibility for the technical delivery of assigned developers.<br><br> Support all stages of the Software development and deployment lifecycle to ensure smooth delivery including design, build, testing, deployment and warranty.<br><br> Assist when required with analysis and resolutions of issues in the production environment. <br><br> Collaborate with Enterprise, Technical and Solutions Architects, Developers, Product Owners, Scrum masters and other stakeholders on a continual basis throughout the software development lifecycle to ensure high quality solutions are designed, built and delivered that adhere to the Architectural principles and processes. <br><br> Liaise closely with Third party software and Infrastructure providers to ensure the quality and suitability of their technical design and solutions including non-functional design and development considerations. Review and challenge coding estimates, challenge code design and collaborate with service provider teams to improve the effectiveness and timeliness of their deliveries<br><br> Ensure Technical documentation of code and within code is accurate, knowledge is shared and the company's intellectual property is safeguarded.<br><br>Liaise closely with IT management to conceive, own and maintain the coding standards/clean coding techniques and principles, develop quality assurance procedures and drive regular reviews and analysis to govern IT policies and coding standards<br><br> Ensure security of data and intellectual property is ensured, without exception and drive reviews and quality checks to ensure data security is at the heart of all development that is being undertaken. <br><br><strong>Skills, Experience &amp; Qualifications:</strong><br> <ul><li>Technical experience developing E-commerce applications using Java/J2EE and comfortable developing web services/microservices architecture.</li><li>Strong Communication, able to assimilate complex technical concepts rapidly and communicate ideas clearly in both written and verbal format to many stakeholders is essential.</li><li>Experience within Insurance or the wider Financial Services industry would be beneficial.</li></ul> Additionally, knowledge of some or all of the following is beneficial:<br> <ul><li>Spring framework (Spring Boot, MVC, Dependency Injection, Data Access)</li><li>JDBC, SQL, XML, Junit, LDAP, Active Directory, Eclipse, Subversion, HTML5, CSS3, Bootstrap, Javascript, JQuery <ul><li>IBM Websphere Application Server/Tomcat</li><li>Web Services (HTTP, ReST, JSON, XML)</li><li>Test-Driven/Behaviour-Driven Development methods and frameworks</li><li>CI/CT/DevOps Tools and Technologies</li><li>Full understanding of: applicable database technologies (DB2, Oracle, SQL Server), performance/clustering/scalability concerns, Data Warehousing and reporting (eg Business Objects, Ab-initio, SAS) and Enterprise content management products.</li><li>Application integration with multiple platforms and data sources (Mainframe, mid-range, SOA, ESB technologies)</li><li>JIRA, Confluence or similar tools</li><li>Application and Web Service security, Identity Management and Protocols (eg OWASP, WS-Security, SAML, OAuth2, OpenID Connect)</li><li>IT Infrastructure (SAN Technologies,basic networking, Windows, Linux, zOS, Cloud architectures</li><li>Knowledge or experience with Cloud Technologies. Azure would be great!</li><li>Agile development methodology, SAFe, SCRUM</li><li>Waterfall Software development lifecycle</li><li>ITIL, TOGAF, PRINCE2 etc</li><li>Managing projects/tasks in a large corporate environment</li></ul> </li></ul> <strong>Qualifications:</strong><br> <ul><ul><li>It is desirable that the Candidate has a degree or equivalent qualification in: IT, computer science, business, engineering, Mathematics or Sciences but experienced Candidates with extensive industry experience are equally of interest. </li><li>Professional industry standard qualifications ie. ITIL, PRINCE2, Certified Scrum Professional (CSP), SAFe Agilist (SA) etc are desirable</li></ul> </ul> Interested Candidates need to apply now and will receive initial feedback on their application within 72 hours. <br><br></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">

</div><div class="visareqtext"></div><div class="clear"></div><div id="md_skills" class="md_skills"><p> <strong>Senior Network Engineer - Hemel Hempstead - £55k + Benefits</strong><br> <br> Our client is a major Telecommunications and Networking provider require a Senior Network Engineer to join their team in Hemel Hempstead. They provide public WiFi service to 100 millions WiFi users across 120,000 UK hotel rooms, 32 airports, London street and many other public sites.<br> <br> <strong>Role Purpose for the Senior Network Engineer:</strong><br> You'll be enthusiastic about modern methods for deployment management and platform delivery, with a pragmatic style and great analytical skills that help you identify and solve problems before our customers do. You will have a keen sense of architecture, security, resilience and performance that allows you to spot solutions that work and those that don't. You'll be continually learning and have an eye on the tech coming over the horizon.<br> <br> <strong>Key Accountabilities for the Senior Network Engineer:</strong></p><ul><li>Project Delivery - Engage within the initial stages of programmes, projects and initiatives. This will feed into the test plan with up to date requirements thus identifying synergies that drive quality across networks and platform upto NOC (Network Operations)</li><li>Tools and Technology - Jira and Confluence for regular defect tracking and other in-build automation tools for regression test execution purpose. Meraki, Mikrotik and Cisco technologies will be used as part of environment build.</li><li>Support -Collaborate with support team manager on acceptance of projects into live environments. Ensures test and deployment compliance with relevant standards eg ITIL, ISTQB and internal/external auditing authorities. Able to take timely action to co-ordinate resolution activity for key risk areas</li><li>Communication - Ensure strong communication processes (written and verbal, IT and customer) are established, concentrating particularly on test and deployment activities. Acting as a test representative for Service validation and deployment area across all levels of the business.</li><li>Culture - Engender a culture of continuous improvement, energy, collaboration and fun across department.</li><li>Career Development - Provide input to people managers to assist with the promotion of career</li><li>Provide support in a deputy capacity where necessary for the Test Manager to ensure continuity of a quality assurance is achieved across test and deployment activities at project level.</li><li>Provide reports on testing results, coverage and make recommendations where necessary.</li></ul><p> <strong>Essential Knowledge, experience and skills for Senior Network Engineer role: </strong></p><ul><li>Define and follow standards and best practices for network design, testing, and implementation methodology. Document different types of network environment.</li><li>Bachelor's degree in Computer Science or other related field or equivalent knowledge with 6-10 years of related professional experience.</li><li>5+ years of direct engineering and design experience in the telecommunications and/or networking industry and/or B2B Internet Space. Cisco CCNP/CCDP or CCIE certifications preferred.</li><li>Understanding of transport protocols, routing protocols, and security/authentication protocols at all layers of the OSI model with emphasis on TCP/IP are essential.</li><li>Subject Matter Expert in IP protocols including BGP, EIGRP, OSPF, IP Multicast, MPLS Proficiency working with VLAN, VRF, HSRP, Port Security, Traffic Shaping, Priority Queuing, Class of Service (CoS)</li><li>Advanced knowledge of enterprise wireless architectures (design, implementation &amp; troubleshooting)</li><li>In depth experience with multiple vendor¹s hardware, including Cisco, Mikrotik, Juniper, Aerohive etc.</li><li>Must have knowledge of networking features and protocols such as spanning tree, ARP, CDP, EIGRP, RIP, OSPF, BGP, VTP, Etherchannel, 802.1Q trunking, MLS, HSRP, QoS, multicast, 802.11, IPsec, Frame Relay, RADIUS/TACACS+, SNMP, T-1/E-1, BRI/PRI, MPLS, Dial-up services, and caching services.</li><li>Experience with network management tools such as Sniffers, Wireshark, Solarwinds etc.</li><li>Experience supporting Windows and UNIX products systems/applications on networking technologies.. Ability to learn new things quickly, and need minimal direction.</li><li>A high degree of creative ability, analytical and technical skills and independent judgment/decision making.</li><li>Good strategic planning, project management, organizational and time management skills to handle multiple complex enterprise-scale complex projects simultaneously.</li><li>Excellent communications and presentation skills and candidate must have the ability to communicate with internal/external customers, vendors, management etc. in both formal and informal situations.</li><li>Strong interpersonal skills needed to team well with peers, customers, project managers, and vendor</li></ul><p>If you are interested in the role and would like to apply, please send me your CV via the link below for immediate consideration.</p><p><strong>Senior Network Engineer - Hemel Hempstead - £55k + Benefits</strong></p><p>Capita IT Resourcing is acting as an Employment Agency in relation to this vacancy.</p></div><!-- skills --><div class="clear"></div><div id="jd_mediaUrl" class="jd_mediaUrl"></div><div class="clear"></div><hr><!-- these are the individual job detail headers (labels and actual job detail) --><div class="md_items">
